et ewe l’enfant selonc la figure natureil, et la fai esternuer, et li comande qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse fuer.	and turn the child according to its natural position, and make her sneeze, and instruct her to hold on until the baby comes out.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus son col, et ait espandues ses mains, et sa faice tornee devers lou dos sa mere	from the child's exit at its neck, and spread his hands, and turned his face towards his mother's back
I covient que li baile teigne sa main, puis le torne poc et poc, et l’ewe legierement;	I must tie her hand, then turn it slowly little by little, and gently;
et quant il est igalz, si met sus la nature muscillaige de altee et oile, si com nos avons dit, puis li comande qu’elle se mueve poc et poc;	and when it is even, then place on the skin a poultice of alder and oil, as we have said, then instruct that it moves little by little.
et quant tu avras ce fait, si la fai seoir sus .i. siege, et li comande k’elle se preigne; et la fai esternuer.	and when you have done this, then make her sit on a chair, and instruct her to sneeze; and make her yawn.
de ceste meisme maniere a tout la secondine	in the same way with all the afterbirth
Quant il vient fuer en ceste maniere a tout la secondine, si cope la secondine a ton ungle, tant que li moistors soit vuidie;	When it comes out in this way at all the afterbirth, then catch the afterbirth with your nail, as long as the moisture is discharged;
et se li enfes pent sus sa faice et sus son col, si la cope des la boude, qu’elle ne soit retenue, et muere li enfes;	and if the child puts its hands on its face and neck, and the mother slaps it, it should not be restrained, and the child will die.
puis boute l’enfant dedens, tant que tu l’aies mis si com il covient, et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne aucune fois:	then put the child inside, as you have placed it as it should be, and instruct the woman to grip several times:
adonques si istra legierement.	then let go gently.
de l’issue des gemelz	of the exit of twins
Saiches que gemeil naissent maintes fois, et aucune fois en naissent .iij. ou .iiij.; et ceu n’est mie estrainge chose, et poc avient.	Know that twins are born many times, and sometimes three or four are born; and this is not a strange thing, and it happens rarely.
Dui sont estrainge chose, et ne vivent mie, se poc nom;	Twins are a strange thing, and do not live long if they are born prematurely.
je sai ceu, qu’il soient multipliiet, et sont desevrez par lou syfac qui les devise, qui est liiez a la boude;	I know that they are multiples, and are separated by the placenta that divides them, which is attached to the womb.
et aucune fois issent ausi naturelment com uns tous sous, si com nos avons dit.	And sometimes they issue naturally as one does, as we have said.
Et s’il issent griement, si la cure si com nos avons dit, et soit li baile subtilz, et faice tost et legierement ceu qu’elle fait;	And if they grow quickly, then the treatment as we have said, and let the nurse be skilled, and do quickly and lightly what she does;
et faice ensi com il vaut mues a salut.	and do thus as it is beneficial for healing.
de plusors enfans	of many children
Aucune fois sont formez en la marris .i. ou .ij. ou .iij. ou .iiij. ou .v. ou .vj. ou .vij., ou plusors jusc’a .xv., et sont tout formeit en forme d’enfant par le mesurement dou saige glorious,	Sometimes they are formed in the womb as one or two or three or four or five or more, up to fifteen, and they are all formed in the shape of a child according to the measurement of the glorious Sage,
et couvient que li baile saiche tout ceu, car par aventure semblans chose li avient;	and it is necessary for the surgeon to know all this, because similar things might happen to him.
si faice selonc ceu qu’il covient.	then he should act accordingly.
de l’enfant mort	of the dead child
Quant tu cures la femme de l’enfant mort ou ventre, si com j’ai dit en la division, et il ne vient fuers, et tu es constrains d’ovraige de mains;	When you are treating a woman of a stillborn child, as I have said in the section on obstetrics, and there is no labor, and you are forced to act manually:
si covient que tu saiches se li femme est de saine vertut, et n’ait accident ou elle ait paor de mort;	if you know that the woman is of sound health and has no fear of death.
si covient que li femme soit sovinee sus son dos, et soit ses chiés enclins aval, et les jambes levees;	it is necessary for the woman to lie on her back, with her hips tilted down and legs raised;
et li ministre la teigne de .ij. pars, ou elle soit liie au lit si qu’elle ne soit traite au dessendement de l’enfant;	and the midwife should apply the unguent of ten parts where she lies in bed so that she is not treated with the descent of the child;
puis frotez la bouche de la marris d’oiles moistes avec muscillaige de altee et de fenugrec et semence de lin, puis oigne li baile ses mains de ces oiles et de ces muscillaiges;	then rub the mouth of the mother with moist oils mixed with myrrh and fenugreek and flax seed, then anoint the midwife's hands with these oils and myrrh;
puis les boute en la marris legierement, puis quiere .i. leu ou elle boute les oncines que soient covenaubles a ceu,	then they beat it lightly, then they pick .I. the place where it beats the joints that are suitable for this,
et pren warde se li enfes est apparilliez qu’il dessende sus son chief;	and take care that the infant is equipped so that he descends onto his head;
si fiche les oncines en ses eulz ou en son col ou en sa bouche ou en som palais ou desoz la barbe ou en la forcele ou pres des costez,	if he strikes the joints in his eyes or throat or mouth or palate or under the beard or near the sides,
et se li dessendemens est sus piez, se li fiche ou poignil et as costes moienes;	and if the descent is on the feet, let him hit or pinch and middle sides;
et covient qu’il teigne l’oncine a sa main destre, et mette la corbeure entre ses dois de la senestre main, et li boute a tout sa main legierement, et fiche l’oncine en aucun de ces leus que nos avons dit, tant qu’il viegne a la chose vuide;	and he should dye the thread with his right hand, and place the needle between the fingers of his left hand, and wind the thread lightly around his hand, and insert the needle into one of the places we have mentioned, so that it reaches the hollow space;
et c’est li forme de l’oncine:	and this is how the needle should be formed:
puis fiche encontre .i. autre oncine, ou le tier se tu en as mestier, si que li estractions soit igalz;	then insert another needle, or a third one if you need it, so that the extractions are equal;
et puis l’estent igalment en movant d’une part et d’autre, por mues issir, et soit li oncines dentez por mues tenir, si com ci est li forme:	and then they should be moved equally from one side to the other, so that they exit, and the needles should be bitten down to hold them in place, as shown in this illustration:
Et s’il en demoure une partie, si oigne li baile aucuns de ses dois d’oile, et les boute en celle partie, et traie l’autre partie;	And if a part remains, then anoint the knuckles of one hand with oil, and rub it into that part, and draw out the other part;
et s’il en i demoure point, si met cest oncine ou plus haut leu, et fai ceu tant qu’il s’en isse tout fuers.	and if nothing remains, then place this finger or a higher one in place, and do this until it all comes out.
Et se l’une mains vient devant l’autre, et il ne puet ramener por l’estreignement,	And if one hand comes before the other, and he cannot bring it back due to the dislocation,
si covient que tu envoloupes sus .i. drapeil, tant qu’il isse tote;	then you must wrap it in .a. cloth, as much as it will go;
puis la cope en la jointure de la plante ou au coute, et ensi covient que tu faices en l’autre main, et as .ij. piés.	then cut at the joints of the fingers or toes, and thus you must do to the other hand, and on both feet.
Et se li chiés de l’enfant est gros et il est estrois en l’issue, ou il ait ou chief aigue assemblee,	And if the head of the child is big and it is stretched out at the exit, or has an acute headache,
si covient que tu boute le spatumile espinous entre tes dois, et fent le chief et estrai l’aigue;	you should press on the spinous process between your fingers, and open the head and draw out the water;
ou tu la ront a l’estrument qui est apelez «almidach», de coi li forme vient avec les estrumens ou chapistre qui est aprés cestui;	or you may use the instrument called "almidach," from which the shape comes with the instruments or chapters that follow this one;
et ensi meisme faice se li enfes a grant chief naturelment;	and likewise, make the infant a large head naturally;
et puis traie fuer les osses as tenailles,	and then pull out the bones with tongs,
et se li chiés saut fuer et il estraint a la forcele, si soit fendus, tant que li moistors qui est ou pis issue fuer;	and if the head pops out and is forced, it should be split open until the moisture that is inside comes out;
et s’elle ne puet issir, si le cope par pieces au mues que tu pues;	and if it cannot come out, then cut it in pieces as much as you can;
et s’il est enflez au ventre ou desoz les costez, si covient que tu lou perces tant que li moistors corre.	and if it is swollen in the belly or beneath the ribs, then you must pierce it so that the moisture flows out.
Et se li enfes est sus ses piez, si est li attraction legiere, et li adrecemens a la bouche de la marris est legier.	And if the swelling is on their feet, the pull is light, and the movement towards the mouth of the wound is easy.
Et s’il est estrois au ventre ou au pis, si couvient que tu l’estraies a .i. drapeil envoloupeit sus la main;	And if it is swollen in the belly or foot, you must stretch it with .i. bandage wrapped around the hand;
et fent le ventre ou le pis, tant que li moistors qui i est corre;	and open the belly or foot, so that the moisture which is in it flows out;
et se li autre membre sont osteit, et li chiez demoure,	and if other limbs are affected, but the feet remain
si boute li baile sa main em parfont de la marris, et le traie jusc’a la bouche de la marris;	if he also puts his hand into the wound and pulls it up to the mouth of the wound;
puis i boute .i. oncine ou ij., et le trai fuer;	then put in a needle or two, and pull them out;
et se li bouche de la marris est retrecie por aposteme chaut qui i est venus, si n’i covient mie travillier,	and if the mouth of the wound is narrowed due to a hot abscess that has formed there, then one should not work on it,
ains covient amenistrer choses moistes et grasses;	then one must apply moist and fatty things;
et li amenistre emplaustres, et siece en aigue mollifians et amoistans.	and apply poultices, and use warm and softening water.
Et se li enfes est sus son costeit, et tu le pues mettre igal, si amenistre ceu que nos avons dit en l’enfant vif;	And if the child is on its side, and you can get it to lie still, then apply what we have said for a living child:
et s’on nen ait pooir, si lou trai fuer par pieces, et n’i laissier rien de la secondine.	and if one cannot, then let it be carried in parts, and leave nothing of the afterbirth.
Et quant tu avras ce fait, se li amenistre ceu que nos avons dit ens apostemes chaus que vienent en la marris;	And when you have done this, if he is given what we have said about abscesses that come in the sea;
et se decorremens de sanc vient, si soit mise en aigue restraignant, et li amenistre autres cures.	and if there is bleeding, let it be stopped with astringents, and other remedies administered.
Et je vis une femme en cui ventre uns enfes avoit esteit mors, puis consut .i. autre sus celui, et refut mors li autres.	And I saw a woman in whose belly a child had died, then another was sewn over it, and the other died too.
Aprés lonc tens li vint uns apostemes en la boude, et enfla tant qu’il ovrit, et comensa a grant porreture.	After a long time she got an abscess in her armpit, which swelled so much that it opened and began to ooze profusely.
je fui apelez a la cure, et i pensai lonc tens, et ne pot soder li plaie.	I was called to the wound, and I thought for a long time, but could not heal it.
Je mis sus emplaustre de fort attraction, et en issit uns os, et aprés aucuns jors uns autres.	I applied a strong attracting plaster, and one bone came out, and after a few days, some others.
Je me mervillai mout, por ceu c’ou ventre n’a point d’os.	I was very amazed, because the belly has no bones.
Si pensai que c’estoit des os d’un enfant mort.	I thought that they were the bones of a dead child.
Je quis la plaie, et en traï mains os, tant que li femme fut em miglior point;	Examine the wound, and with your hands pull out the bones until the woman is in a better state.
et vesquit li femme lonc tens ensi, et issoit adés un poc de bowe dou leu;	and let the woman rest like this for a long time, and then slowly move her neck a little;
et je n’ai recordeit cest chapistre fuer que por ceu que, quant li maistres trueve une estrainge chose, qu’il i saiche mettre aide.	and I have not mentioned this chapter before because, when the masters encounter an unusual case, they will know how to provide assistance.
dou ramener la marris a son leu	how to return the dislocated joint to its place
Ci aprés vient li forme dou pressor, a coi on ewe les livres; et a .ij. tornans as .ij. chiés des .ij. liiens.	Hereafter comes the form of the press, with which one cuts into the books; and in .2 turns at .2 ears of .2 lines.
Toutevoie, li cornes soit plus subtilz dou restrictoire, et soit fais de ebene ou de bux;	Nevertheless, let the horns be more subtle of the constrictor, and be made of boxwood or of ebony;
et soit li bouche dou fust .i. doi de large, et li marge des arbres .i. doit, et de lonc une palme et demi;	and let the mouth of the pipe be one digit wide, and the edges of the trees one digit, and in length one palm and a half;
et enmi les .ij. liemens soient dui ajostemens de cest meisme fust, qui soient fermeit en l’un et en l’autre, de demi palme de lonc ou un poc plus;	and in the .2 sides are two adjustments of this same wood, which are fastened in one and the other, half a palm long or a little more;
et cist dui ajostement sont bouteit en la bouche de la marris por ovrir quant on torne les .ij. cornes.	and these two settings are put into the mouth of the wound to open when you turn the two horns.
Une autre forme, a sa semblance plus subtilz et plus legiere, soit faite de fust de ebene ou de bux, selonc la semblance des tenailles;	Another form, more subtle and lighter, is made of boxwood or box, according to the appearance of tweezers;
et ait as .ij. chiés .ij. ajostemens, si com tu vois, d’une palme de lonc, et .ij. dois de large;	and has two heads two settings, as you see, a palm long, and two fingers wide;
et quant tu vues ovrir la marris a tout l’estrument, si fai seoir la femme sor .i. lit, les piez pendant et les jambes overtes,	and when you see the wound open to all the instrument, so let the woman sit on a bed, her feet hanging and her legs spread,
puis boute les .ij. ajostemens ajostez ensamble en la marris, et tien le chief de l’estrument desoz entre ses cuixes;	then put the two pieces of the instrument together in the socket, and hold the head of the instrument under between his thighs;
puis oevre ta main a tout l’estrument, si com tu as fait as tenailles igalment, selonc la quantiteit que tu vues ovrir la bouche de la marris, tant que li baile faice ceu qu’elle vuet.	then work your hand on the whole instrument, just as you did with the tongs, according to the amount that you see opening the mouth of the socket, until the patient does what he wants.
Cist estrument sont tuit sormontez, et sont multiplies lor semblances; et quant li mires les ait apareilliez, tant est plus hastans li oevre, et plus haute as homes por lor quantiteit.	These instruments are all decorated, and their appearances are multiplied; and when the patient sees them prepared, his fear is increased, and he is more reluctant to undergo the procedure because of their quantity.
Si ne despire mie l’estrument que tu ne l’aies apparelliet, car lor necessitez n’est mie escusauble.	Do not despair about the instrument until you have prepared it, for their necessity is unavoidable.
Quant li secondine est retenue a l’enfantement, si covient que tu comandes a la malaide qu’ele reteigne son alaine, et puis la fai esternuer de condisi, et li estraint tes mains a la bouche et au neis;	When the afterbirth is retained at childbirth, you must instruct the patient to hold in her breath, then make her sneeze with an herb, and squeeze her hands to her mouth and nose.
et s’elle saut per ceu, bien est.	And if she vomits, that's good.
Se ceu non, si prent .i. pot, et fai .i. pertus ou cuvercle, et i met herbes que puissent ovrir la bouche de la marris, si com calament, rue, anis, camomille, cassialigne et centoire;	If not, take a jug and put herbs that can open the mouth of the womb, such as calendula, anise, chamomile, cassia, and centaury.
toutes ces herbes, ou aucunes d’eles, soient cuites ou pot en aigue sus le feu; puis met une caine ou pertus dou pot, et l’autre chief en la bouche de la marris,	All of these herbs, or some of them, are cooked in water over the fire. Then put one end of the tube into the jug and the other end into the mouth of the womb,
et la teigne tant que li vapors viegne dedens la marris; puis la fai esternuer, si com nos avons dit.	and the dye until the vapor comes inside the marble; then let it sneeze, as we have said.
Si saut li secondine hastanment.	Then let the secondine dry quickly.
Et s’elle remaint aprés ceste cure, et n’ist mie fuer, si comande a la baile qu’ele moille sa main senestre en oile de sesement ou en muscillaige de altee, et puis la boute en la nature,	And if it remains after this treatment and is not better, command the bather to wet her left hand in oil of sesame or in a poultice of alder, and then let her put it back in its natural place,
et quiere la secondine; et quant elle l’avra trovee, si la preigne et l’estende poc et poc droitement, si que li marris ne chiece a l’estraction;	and seek the secondine; and when she has found it, she should grip and gradually stretch it straight, so that the marble does not pop out.
mais la covient movoir legierement a destre et a senestre, et puis traie; si venra et se desaerdra.	but it must be moved slightly to the right and left, and then pulled; thus it will come out and loosen.
Et se li bouche de la marris est jai estrecie, nos avons dit la cure d’esternuer, et de fumigation des herbes;	And if the opening of the wound is narrow, we have described the treatment of sneezing and the fume of herbs;
et s’elle n’ist de tout ceu que nos avons dit, si garde que tu ne foloies au traire;	and if it is not one of those that we have described, then beware of pulling;
mais il couvient que ceu qui est a la bouche de la marris, que tu le lies a la cuixe de la femme, puis la clisterize d’oignement tetrafarmaçon;	but it is necessary for the person at the mouth of the wound to tie it to the woman's thigh, then cleanse it with tetrafarmacon ointment;
si la porrira et remettra, et venra fuer; mais toutevoie, quant elle porrist si en vient male odor au stomac et au chief, et blece la malaide.	if she vomits it up and expels it, but nonetheless, when she vomits it comes out with a bad smell from the stomach and head, and weakens the patient.
Si covient donques fumigations covenaubles a ceu: aucun des anciens ont esproveit fumigation de cresson et de figues seches.	So then one should use appropriate fume: some of the ancients have tried smoke from watercress and dry figs.
Li forme de l’estrument a coi on fumige la femme a la retenue des flors et de la secondine si est ceste:	The shape of the instrument used to smoke out the woman for the retention of flowers and afterbirth is as follows:
Et est de voirre semblant a une caine, et met on le chief subtil en la nature, et les chiés larges sus le feu;	And it is made of glass like a tube, and one puts the narrow end into the woman's birth canal, and the wide end above the fire;
et soit li fumigations sus les charbons, et la teigne tant qu’elle soit gastee, et rencomence une autre.	and let him use fomentation on the charcoal, and the dye until it is wasted, and begin another.
de percier lou fondement	to pierce the foundation
Maint enfant naissent qui n’ont mie le fondement perciet, ains l’ait estoupeit uns subtilz syfac:	Many children are born who do not have the foundation pierced, but instead have a thin, subtle membrane.
si covient donques a la baile qu’ele perce celui syfac a son doit, et ne lou perce mie de spatumile agut, et garse le lacement qu’elle ne le touche;	Therefore, it is necessary for the midwife to pierce this membrane with her finger, and not cut it with a knife, and guard against tying it off so that she does not touch it.
puis met sus lainne moillie en vin et en oile, puis la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	then put on soft lamb's wool soaked in wine and oil, then dress the wound with ointment until it is healed.
Et se tu doutes qu’il ne restoupe, si met ou pertus une caine de plonc, et li laisse mains jors, et soit ostee quant li enfes vuet aler en chambres.	And if you doubt that he will be cured, then put a plug of wool in the wound, and leave it for several days, and remove it when the child wants to go to bed.
Et aucune fois vient cist estoupemens de soudement de plaie ou d’aposteme; si covient coper celui soudement: si soit curez, si com nos avons dit de la caine de plonc.	And sometimes a sudden stop to the bleeding occurs in a wound or an abscess; then it must be stopped suddenly: then it should be dressed as we have said with a plug of wool.
de la fistule dou fondement	from the fistula of the fundament
Fistules qui vienent desoz le fondement sont nodation, et groissor que vienent delez lou fondement defuer, ou en l’espaice des .ij. parties,	Fistulas that come from under the anus are nodular, and grow larger than those that come from within the anus, or in the space of the two parts.
si a une fistule ou plusors; et quant celle nodation est anciene, si aoeuvre, et encort moistor awouse blainche ou subtilz bowe,	if there is one fistula or several; and when the nodule is old, it opens, and usually white moisture or thin pus flows out,
et aucune fois sont ces fistule persans; et sont conues par ceu qu’il en ist ou egestion ou ventositeit quant li malaide fait egestion, et par aventure en saut uns vers.	and sometimes these fistulas are piercing; and they are caused by what comes out of the anus or through flatulence when the patient expels gas, and sometimes a small one pops out.
Et si a fistules que percent jusc’a la vessie, et jusc’a la moitiet de la verge; et parvienent jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, et jusc’a nout de la kowe.	And there are fistulas that pierce all the way to the bladder, and halfway down the shaft of the penis; and they reach up to the hip joint, and to the scrotum.
Et ensi conoist on la fistule persant au fondement, et ne mie persant:	And thus one knows the fistula that flows from the anus and does not flow:
et est que tu boutes ton doi indice ou fondement, et boute une aguille subtil d’arain ou de fer en la fistule quant il n’i a tortuositeit.	and put your index finger into the anus, and insert a thin needle of copper or iron into the fistula when there is no curvature.
Et s’il ait tortuositeit, si i boute une tente de plonc subtil, ou .i. poil de cheval, tant que tu sentes la tente ou le poil a ton doit;	And if it has a curve, insert a thin tent or horsehair until you feel the tent or hair at your finger;
et se tu ne le sens, et il ne vient dou pertus egestion ne ventositeit ne ver, si com nos avons dit:	and if you do not feel it and no pus, gas, or diarrhea comes out, as we have said:
saiches qu’elle ne perce mie; si te haste dou curer.	so that it does not pierce through; then hasten to treat it.
Et quant li fistule est persans jusc’a la vessie ou jusc’a conduit de l’urine, si en saut li urine, et ne puet soudeir par medicines.	And when the fistula has reached the bladder or the urethra, then the urine flows out, and medicine cannot stop it.
S’elle est percie jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, si est li tente venans jusc’au leu;	If it has pierced through to the hip joint, then the tent will draw blood from that spot.
s’il n’i a tortuositeit et li invention de la dolor entor, si est qu’il en ist adés bowe, et n’i vaut medicine ne soudement par oignement;	If there is twisting and pain in the joint, and it remains swollen, then medicine and poultices are of no use.
et en ces fistules persans n’a point de cure fuer que labor, et vaniteit des folz mires qui s’en entremettent.	and in these persian fistulas there is no cure for the labor, and vanity of the foolish mirrors that intervene.
En celle qui n’est mie persans et n’est mie anciene, a esperance de saniteit par fer, si com j’ai esproveit,	In that which is not Persian and is not old, there is hope of healing by iron, as I have experienced.
et est que li malaides gise entre tes mains sus son dos; et li lieve les jambes jusque sus ses cuixes, et ait ses cuixes enclinees a son ventre;	and the patient lies on his back; and he lifts his legs up to his thighs, and has his thighs tilted towards his belly;
puis boute une tente d’arain, ou de plonc s’il i a tortuositeit, tant que tu saiches ou li tente vient.	then insert a tent made of iron or lead, if there is tortuosity, as far as you know the tent goes.
Se li malaides la sent entor le fondement, si covient que tu i boutes ton doi indice,	If the pain is felt around the anus, you must insert your finger.
se sens adonques que li tente l’ait perciet; et soit descoverte ou tu sens entre ton doit le syfac ou la char, adonques saiches qu’elle est persans;	and feel if the rectum has been perforated; and if it is uncovered where you feel between your finger and the anus, then know that it is perforated;
si n’i travillier mie c’on ne la puet saner.	if one does not work on it, it cannot be healed.
On dist toutevoie c’on em puet bien saner aucuns, mais ce avient poc;	One says nevertheless that some can be healed well, but this happens rarely;
et li aide c’on i fait, si est c’on eschaufe le cautere subtil selonc la largesce de la fistule, si com il est devant dit;	and the help one does, then one scorches the delicate cautery according to the size of the fistula, as it is said before;
et le boute tout chaut en la fistule, tant qu’il viegne delez le fondement; et faice ceu .ij. fois ou .iij., tant que tu saiches que ces chars fautrees soient arses, qui sont semblant a une penne d’oiseil;	and insert it hot into the fistula, as far as the anus; and do this .ii. or .iii. times, until you know that these charred materials are burned, which look like a bird's feather;
et puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre, tant que celle chars isse fuer, puis le cure d’oignement enjanrant char et soudant.	and then treat it with moist bandages smeared with butter, until the charred materials come out, and then treat it with ointment that softens and binds.
S’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien. Se ceu, nom autrement ne puet estre sanez;	If he is thus healed, it is good. If not, then it cannot be healed any other way;
et se li tente entre, et ne perce jusc’au doit qui est ou fondement, et a entre ton doi et la tente une coverture espesse de char ou de syfac, et tu vois la fistule a ceu qui enseut la coverture dou keur;	and if it enters the tent and does not pierce all the way through to the bottom, which is at the foundation, and there is between your finger and the tent a thick covering of flesh or skin, and you see the fistula following the covering of the heart;
si le cope des l’encomencement de la fistule, et boute adés avant la tente, et pues le cautere aprés, tant qu’il viegne au chief de la tente;	if he cuts at the beginning of the fistula, and then blocks it off in front of the tent, and then cauterizes afterwards, until it reaches the top of the tent;
et sera delivré li tente, et cherra; puis mondefie celles chars fautrees que semblent une penne d’oisel, et n’en remaigne niant.	and the tent will be delivered, and fall down; then cut off those false pieces of flesh that look like a bird's feather, and nothing remains.
Et si li sans te vaint, et cort entre toi et l’uevre, si le cauterize de feu ou de medicine ague.	And if the pus runs out, and goes between you and the wound, then cauterize it with fire or with medicine.
Car li cauteres de feu assemble .ij. bones choses: c’est a savoir, l’arsure de ces chars ajostees, et l’esteinchement de sanc et la sechor de la moistor;	For fire cautery gathers together two things: that is to say, the scorching of these heated bodies, and the stanching of blood and the drying up of moisture.
puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre ou en choz broiez, tant que li leus giete bowe, et isse fuer li chars arse en la bowe;	Then dress the tent with butter or pounded substance until the place weeps, and let the fire burn in the bow.
puis cure la plaie des oignemens soudans enjanrans dure char, et sont les medicines seches.	Then treat the wound with sudatory, hard, dry remedies.
Car quant il est restoree, si est sanee et ne revient mie.	For when it is restored, it is healed and does not return.
Et se fistule vient jusc’a parfont dou fondement, et est esloigniez dou cors, se li boute ton doi ou fondement, et enquier ceu.	And if a fistula comes from the depth of the foundation, and is separated from the body, put your finger into it, and explore it.
Se tu sens la tente, et entre .ij. est li toile ou li syfac ou chars, ou il est pres a percier, si n’i ait fuers que voie de fiance et d’esperance, par l’aministrement de l’une des .iii. manieres:	If you feel the tent, and between them is the membrane or skin, or it is close to piercing, then do not have fears that show no hope or expectation through the administration of one of the three methods:
ou tu le cauterizes si com nos avons dit, ou tu le cope jusc’a fons, ou se tu pues si i met tentes et cure si com premier;	either you cauterize it as we have said, or cut it to the bottom, or if you can, put in tent and cure as first described;
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que tu ne coper le tenement qui tient le fondement, et viegne li egestions par lai sens volenteit;	and do not go too deep, so that you do not cut the membrane that holds the foundation, and let the discharge come out through there as it wants to;
puis le cure, si com nos avons dit;	then treat, as we have said;
par aventure si sera sanez, ou tu esloigne celle coverture et la munde puis qu’elle est copee delez lou fondement, ou par tente ou par autre estrument apointé;	by chance if it is cured, or you remove that covering and clean it after it has been cut away from the foundation, either by tenting or by another pointed instrument;
puis mondefie cele char fautree qui est en la plaie, tant com tu pues;	then probe the wound, as much as you can;
puis estudie a restorer la plaie, et a demorer la fistule en la partie defuers le fondement: si iert plus legiere chose au malaide.	then treat to close the wound and stop the fistula in the part above the foundation: if it is easier for the patient.
Et aucune fois sont fistules selonc ceste maniere: et est quant tu boutes la tente en la fistule, et elle est ou costeit dou fondement delez lou cuir desus,	And sometimes there are fistulas according to this manner: and it is when you put the tent in the fistula, and it is on the side of the foundation below the skin above,
si pren une tente percie au chief selonc ceste forme:	take a tent pierced at the top according to this shape:
Et i boute .i. fil tort en .ij., et boute la tente a tout le fil en la fistule tant qu’il soit au chief.	And he inserts a twisted thread into it, and inserts the tent along the entire thread into the fistula as far as the top.
S’elle est persans en la marge dou fondement dedens, adonc estrai lou fil de celui pertus, ensi que tu boutes ton doi ou fondement;	If it is piercing in the margin of the foundation inside, then pull out the thread from that hole, just as you would put your finger on the foundation;
et trai le chief dou fil, et assemble les .ij. chiés ensamble, et estraint l’un a l’autre, et le laisse .i. jor ou .ij.;	And draw the head of the thread, and bring together the two heads, and hold them firmly, and leave it for one or two days;
et le restraint aucune fois, tant que li filz cope ces chars que sont entre dous, et chiecent;	and then restrain it again, as long as the threads that are between the two, become tight and tense;
puis cure la plaie tant qu’elle soit soudee et sanee.	then heal the wound until it is healed and clean.
Se li fistule ne perce, si la fai percier en toutes les manieres que tu pues, s’ele n’est trop em parfont.	If the fistula does not drain, then have it drained in every way you can, if it is not too deep.
Car il ne covient mie faire por le lacement coper si em parfont, et puis le cure, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	For it is not appropriate to cover with a bandage immediately after lancing, and then treat the wound, as we have said, until it has healed.
Li forme dou spatumile espinous dont on fent la fistule si est mout agus d’une, part et trenchans;	The form of the spiny spatulum, from which they make a fistula, is very sharp and pointed at one end;
et d’autre part non, por ceu c’on ne cope mie ceu c’on ne doit mie copeir, si com tu vois ci:	and at the other end it is not, so that one should not bandage it, as you will see below:
des emorroydes	of hemorrhoids
Emorrydes sont selonc ij. manieres: ou elles sont dedens le fondement, ausi com grain de resin, et s’en i a petites et grans, et en cort adés sanc,	Hemorrhoids are of two types: they can be inside the anus, like grains of resin, and there are small and large ones, and they ooze blood.
et s’en i a une ou plusors, et sont defuer le fondement et au chief dou fondement; mais celles qui sont defuer si ont poc de moistor,	There can be one or more of them, and they can be either inside the anus or at its opening; but those that are outside have less moisture.and their blood is darker in color. Si li sang est noir, il est cause de coler, et si li sang est rosi, il est cause de coler flegmatique, si li sang est sanguine, il est cause de coler sanguine, si li sang est verd, il est cause de coler melencolique.
et encort adés ou un poc d’aigue citrine ou un poc de sanc, et ont la color dou cors;	If the blood is black, it is caused by a choleric temperament, and if it is reddish, it is caused by a phlegmatic temperament, and if it is bloody, it is caused by a sanguine temperament, and if it is green, it is caused by a melancholic temperament.and they have the color of the body;
et li cure de ces qui les ont dedens le fondement, si est que tu comandes au malaide qu’il s’espreigne por aleir en chambres, tant que li fondemens li isse fuer, et c’aperent li filz;	And the treatment for those who have them inside the anus is that you instruct the patient to strain while going to the toilet until the hemorrhoids come out, and they will hang like threads;
si te haste, et le pent as tenailles, ou tu le tien a ton ungle, puis le cope en ses racines;	If you are in a hurry, grab it with tweezers or your fingernail, then pull out its roots.
et se li uncine ne les pueent tenir por ses moistors, si les prent a .i. drapeil, ou a couton, ou d’une piece de chamelot;	And if the tweezers cannot hold it because of moisture, take it with a piece of cloth or cotton or a piece of chamois leather;
et les estrai a tes dois, puis les cope, et poudre desus aucunes chaudes poudres que soient en leu de cautere;	And pluck them out with your fingers, then pull them out and powder some warm powders on top that act like a cautery;
ou tu les cauterize si com il est dit ou chapistre de cautere, puis les cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez;	Or you can cauterize them as described in the chapter on cauteries, then treat with other treatments until they are healed;The following text is a medieval medical treatise written in Old French, around the 12th-13th centuries.
et se li fondemens ne puet issir, si clisterize le malaide de clistere mordant et aspre por laver ceu qui est ou fondement, si qu’il puist issir apertement;	and if the fundament cannot emerge, then cleanse the patient with a sharp and rough enema to wash away what is in the fundament so that it can emerge openly;
cant li malaides se preint, et se li fil sont fuer dou fondement, si est li cure legiere;	then the patient defecates, and if the thread has come out from the anus, then the cure is easy;
et est que tu les preignes a ton ungle ou as tenailles, et les cope, puis les cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez, et qu’il redoute l’incision par fer.	and you should grasp them with your nail or tweezers and cut them, then treat them as we have said, until they are healed and fear the incision by iron.
Si covient que tu amenistre la costure selonc ceste maniere: pren .i. fil tort, et le boute en une aguille, et puis trai le fil au desus et fai percier l’aguille d’autre part, et torne les .ij. chiez dou fil desoz l’aguille,	If you need to perform sutures in this way: take a twisted thread and thread it through a needle, then pull the thread so that the needle goes through from one side, and return the two ends of the thread under the needle,
et si soit dou large; et estraint le fil forment, puis noe le fil, et estrai l’aguille, et fai ensi de toz les autres, et en laisse .i. por corre la superfluiteit dou sanc;	and if it is too large; tighten the thread tightly, then tie a knot in the thread, and remove the needle, and do likewise with all the others, and leave one to stop the flow of blood;
puis met sus le fondement .i. drapeil moilliet en oile roset ou en cerote, et met sus le fondement, et comande au malaide k’il repose;	then place on the wound a damp cloth soaked in rose oil or in cerate, and place it on the wound, and instruct the patient to rest;
et puis le laisse tant qu’il chiecent, et quant il seront cheut, si les cure d’oignement et d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and then leave him until he defecates, and when he has defecated, then cleanse him with ointment and other remedies until he is healed.
dou sechement dou fiens ou fondement	from dryness of the anus or rectum
Maintes fois avient sechement de fiens en l’intestine, et par constrignement de nature, et quant li maladie est vielle et medicine n’i vaut.	Many times there is dryness of the bowels within the intestines, caused by natural constriction, and when the disease is old and medicine does not help.
Si covient que tu reses a la point d’un spatumile ou a ton ungle l’escorce desus, qui ne le laisse a moistir;	You should cut it with a scalpel or your fingernail to break the skin, so that moisture does not get in.
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sodez si com il covient;	Then dry it until it is hard, as it should be.
et s’il ne puet soder, si rencomence la rasure plus fort que devant, tant qu’il saine mout, et soit escorchiez;	And if it cannot harden, then restart the scraping more aggressively than before, until it heals and is scoured.
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	then treat until healed.
dou fremit	when it trembles
Formice est une petite apparance fautree antor le cors, et va mout em parfont;	A flea is a small creature that creeps under the skin and goes very deeply.
et aucune fois la trueve li frois, et le sent on ausi comme mort de fremit, et vient en tout le cors, et plus as mains que autre part.	And sometimes the flea bites, and one feels it like a trembling, and it comes all over the body, more so in the hands than anywhere else.
Et li cure si est que tu pren une cainne d’une penne d’oie, ou une penne de vultul fort, et met celle caine sus le fremit, tant que li cercles porpreigne le fremit tot entor;	And the cure is that you take a candle made from goose fat, or the fat of a wild goose, and place this candle on the shins, so that the purple circle covers the shins all around.
puis torne ta main a tout la cainne tant que tu copes tout entor le fremit, et le met em parfont, et esraiche le fremit de ses racines.	Then return your hand to the entire candle, so that you cup it all around the shins, and immerse it deeply, and draw out the shin from its roots.
Et se tu vues, si fai ceu d’une caine d’arain ou de fer selonc ceste forme, et soit subtilz desoz et traians desus:	And if you see fit to make a candle of bronze or iron according to this shape, let it be thin beneath and drawn out on top.
ne mie perciet, por mues tenir au doi, et mues presser Et se tu vues, si cauterize lou fremit, si com il est devant ou chapistre de cautere.	Do not pierce it, so that the candle can be held in the hand and pressed against the shin. And if you see fit, cauterize the shins as described in the chapter on cautery.
de la forme dou clistere	of the form of the enema
Aucune fois fait on clistere d’argent ou d’archaut, ou d’arain fondut ou mailliet; et aucune fois fait on de ces estrumens petis et grans, selonc ces a cui il sont amenistrez.	Sometimes an enema is made of silver or brass, or of melted or hammered copper; and sometimes they are made of small and large instruments, depending on those to whom they are administered.
Cil donques c’on amenistre en la cure des enfans et qui sont foible et dolorous, sont petis.	Those who are administered for the treatment of children, and who are weak and painful, are small.
Li forme dou clistere petit et grant si est desus large, ou li ventres est liiez selonc ceste maniere:	The form of the small and large enema is above wide, or the belly is bound according to this manner:
et i ait une desevrance ou li ventres soit liiez, si com tu vois, et li chiez soit dedens perciez; et ait a l’un des costez .ij. pertus, et en l’autre .i.;	and it has a protrusion where the belly is bound, as you can see, and the anus is pierced inside; and it has two openings on one side, and one on the other;
et soit li ventres ou om met les medicines d’une vessie de beste ou de parchemin, et soit perciez tout entor de menus pertus,	and the belly where one puts the medicine is made of a beast's bladder or parchment, and it is pierced all around with small holes;
et ait entre chescun pertus .i. doit d’espaice, puis boute en ces pertus .i. fil fort de fil crut tort en .x. ou enqui entor, et assemble le ventre si com est une chievre;	and it has between each hole a distance of one finger width, then tie into these holes a strong thread of twisted horse hair in a spiral, and assemble the belly so that it is like a goat;
et quant li medicine est dedens, si la lie a l’estrument devant d’un fil fort, puis clisterize; et c’est li forme dou cercle:	and when the medicine is inside, tie it to the instrument in front with a strong thread, then cauterize; and this is the shape of the circle:
Et soit li medicine ne trop chaude ne trop froide, et oint le chief dou clistere d’oile ou d’aubun d’uef, ou de semblant chose, puis le boute ens legierement;	Let the medicine be neither too hot nor too cold, and anoint the head of the syringe with oil or egg white, or similar substance, then insert it gently;
puis l’espreigne li ministres a ses .ij. mains ensamble, tant qu’il soit toz vuis, puis estrai lou clistere, et lieve li malaides ses jambes a la paroit,	then the minister squeezes both ends of the syringe together so that it is empty, then removes the syringe and leaves the patient's legs exposed,
et se li medicine vuet issir, si la teigne tant com il puet; et s’il dort une nuit atot, si est plus grans aide.	and if the medicine wants to come out, let him squeeze as much as he can; and if he sleeps for a night afterwards, it is of greater help.
Et se tu le clisterizes em maladie de decorrement de ventre, et li medicine se haste d’issir, si le rencomence tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if you treat him with a syringe for dysentery, and the medicine rushes out quickly, then repeat it until he is healed.
Et se li emorroide sont ou fondement, ou aposteme, si soit li clistere ausi subtilz com por .i. enfant;	And if hemorrhoids are in the anus or an abscess, then the enema should be as subtle as for a child;
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil sus coi li cuir soit estraint:	and this is the form of the subtle enema that tightens the skin:
des plaies	of wounds
Nos avons jai dit en la division la cure des plaies; or vos dirons les cures de mains et de medicine, selonc l’acomplissement.	We have already discussed in the division the treatment of wounds; now we will discuss manual and medicinal treatments according to their properties.
Je dis que les plaies sont diverses selonc ceu qu’elles sont faites, et selonc les leus ou les plaies sont faites, et de coi elles sont faites.	I say that wounds are diverse according to how they are made, and according to the places where the wounds are made, and according to what makes them.
Les choses par coi plaies sont faites sont par gitement de piere, et taille d’espee et de couteil, ou de lance ou de fust ou de siette, ou de semblans choses;	The objects that cause wounds are by stone-throwing, and sword and knife cuts, or spear, staff, arrow, or similar things;
ou que sont faites selonc les leus dou cors, si com plaie que chiet sus le col, ou sus le chief, ou le peis, ou le ventre, ou le foie, et semblans membres;	or according to the places on the body where they are made, like a wound that falls on the neck, or head, or leg, or belly, or liver, and similar members;
et je vos dirai la cure de chescune plaie, et encomencerai as plaies dou chief simples, car li remenbrance venra en son chapistre.	and I will tell you the treatment for each wound, and I will begin with simple head wounds, because the memory will come in its chapter.
Je dis que quant simple plaie vient ou chief, et li os n’est brisiez, si pren garde se c’est de gitement de piere ou de semblans choses, et li cuir est toutevoie rompus et est li plaie grans,	I say that when a simple wound comes to the head, and the bone is not broken, one should take care if it is from a stone or similar object, and the skin is still intact but the wound is large,
et tu doutes levement d’aposteme chaut: si le fai tantost sainier de la cephalique meismement s’il vient poc de sanc de la plaie, et soit li sainie au contraire de la partie navree;	and you suspect a hot abscess: then have the patient bleed from the cephalic vein immediately if there is little blood coming from the wound, and let the bleeding be in the opposite direction to the wounded part;
et eschuisse li malaides repletion de vin et de viandes grosses.	and reduce the patient's intake of wine and rich foods.
Et s’il ne vuet sainier, si soit amenuisie sa viande, et ne boive point de vin, ne ne menjuce point de char;	And if he does not want to bleed, then his food should be reduced, and he should not drink wine nor eat meat;
et met sor la plaie, se apostemes chaus i vient, coton moilliet en oile roset soulement, ou en vin stiptice;	and place a poultice on the wound, if hot abscesses arise, with cotton moistened only in rose oil or in styptic wine;
et s’il n’i a aposteme chaut, si met sus la plaie, s’elle est fresche a tout son sanc, et elle n’est muee par l’air, poudre, que je dirai un poc ci aprés;	and if there is no hot abscess, then place on the wound, if it is fresh and bleeding, and has not been moved by the wind, a powder which I will describe shortly.
et se li ars l’ait muee, si met sus aucuns oignemens, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and if the wound has been moved by the wind, then place on it some ointments until it is healed.
Et se li plaie est grans si com de tailleure d’espee et de semblans, et les levres ne se pueent assembler par tentes, si les assemble par cousture, si com je dirai as plaies dou ventre, de la costure.	And if the wound is large, such as from a sword cut and similar, and the lips cannot be brought together with stitches, then bring them together with sutures, as I will describe for wounds of the abdomen, of the chest.
Se li plaie est descoverte de l’os, et pent, et ne tient mais que a un poc, si le cope; puis cure la plaie de medicine, et restoure char dure en leu de cuir,	If the wound is exposed to the bone, and it can be covered, and holds only by a little, then treat the wound with medicine, and restore hard flesh in place of skin,
et comande au malaide a mengier grosses viandes, si com testes et froment cuit, ausi com poulz, et semblans choses.	and instruct the patient to eat coarse foods, such as testicles and cooked wheat, as well as meat, and similar things.
Et se tu trueves ou cuir porriture, et il n’aert a l’os, si cope lou porrit tot, et giete fuer, puis le cure;	And if you find pus in the skin, and it is not near the bone, then scoop out all the pus and pour it out, then treat the wound.
et se il ait artere en la plaie ou voine, dont sans cort, et il ne puet estainchier par medicines, si quier l’artere, et se tu la trueves desloie, si la lie d’un fil;	And if there is an artery in the wound or vein, from which blood flows, and it cannot be staunched by medicine, then tie off the artery, and if you find it swollen, then cut into it;
et se ceu ne profite mie, si la cauterize.	and if this does not help, cauterize it.
Et se ces plaies sont petites et simples, si est li cure legiere: et est que tu mettes ens ceste poudre qui soude ainsois que li ars l’ait muee.	And if these wounds are small and simple, then the treatment is easy; you should apply this powder which causes sores to heal as soon as the fire has burned them.
Et li maniere de la poudre si est: pren encens une partie; sanc de dragon .ij. parties; chalz vive .iij. parties, et le poudre subtilment,	And the method of making the powder is as follows: take incense one part, dragon's blood two parts, quicklime three parts, and grind them together finely.
et emple la plaie, et l’estraint forment, tant qu’elle s’aerse bien et se joigne a tout son sanc;	and apply it to the wound, pressing firmly until the wound heals and joins back together with its blood.
et puis la lie bien, et la laisse sens desliier, s’elle n’enfle; car on n’oste la madicine tant qu’ele soit sanee.	and then bind it well and leave it untied if it doesn't swell, for one does not remove the medicine until the wound is healed.
Et aucune fois fait on ceu de chalz soulement, quant on n’ait l’encens ne lou sanc de dragon, mais que li ars n’ait muee la plaie.	And sometimes one makes it only with chalk, when one doesn't have incense or dragon's blood, but so long as the wound is moved by fire.
Et se li ars ait mueit la plaie, meismement en esteit, si n’i met om mie ceste poudre;	And if the wound has been moved by the fire, one should put this powder into it;
mais met sus aucuns oignemens digestis, ou poulz de farine d’orge faites d’aigue et de miel, tant qu’ele giete bowe;	but apply some digestive ointments, or barley flour made with water and honey, until it becomes swollen;
puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	then treat other wounds until he is healed.
Et se li brisure d’os vient avec la plaie, et elle est petite, si l’estrai as pinceures subtilz;	And if the bone fracture comes with the wound, and it is small, then extract it with fine pincers;
et je vos dirai ci aprés les brisures dou chief.	and I will tell you about fractures of the head later.
de la plaie dou col	wounds to the neck
Se plaie vient ou col et elle est simple, si n’a point de difference entre li et celi dou chief, mais se li ners dou col ou li artere est copee.	If the wound is on the neck and it is simple, there is no difference between it and that of the head, but if the nerves of the neck or the artery are cut.
Se c’est li ners, si n’i a autre engien que laissier la cure, et n’i mettre nulle chose restraignant, car il nuit as ners et les fait retraire;	If it is the nerve, there is nothing else to do but to let it be and not put anything restraining on it, because it hurts the nerves and makes them retract.
et ne mettre sus la plaie rien froit, car li substance des ners est froide, et li continuation d’aus si est avec le cerveil, qui est li plus haus membres;	And do not put anything cold on the wound, because the substance of the nerves is cold, and their continuance is with the brain, which is the highest member.
mais soit li medicine souez, si com chalz lavee en aigue douce, et mellee avec oile roset, et cucie lavee ausi en aigue douce,	But let there be medicine on it, such as a poultice of chamomile washed in warm water and mixed with rose oil, and a poultice of cucumber also washed in warm water.
et autres pieres de mine selonc ceste maniere, et oignemens moistes.	and other wet stones, according to this method.
Et se li plaie est grans, si la cout et lie de bendes, puis la cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the wound is large, then cut and ligate the vessels, then treat it until it heals.
Et se les plaies sont parfondes et ele est chevee et pleinne de bowe, si la perce ou plus bas leu;	And if the wounds are deep and she is pregnant and full of bowels, then pierce her or cut lower down.
et se li artere est copee, et decorremens de sanc en vient, si la desoivre, et la loie, et la cauterize se mestier est;	and if the artery is cut and bleeding occurs, then ligate it, and if necessary, cauterize it.
et se li espinee de la gorge est copee, ou li keurs, et li conduiz est gardez, par coi la viande va,	and if the spine of the throat is cut, or the carotid artery, and the windpipe is preserved, through which food passes,
si cout le keur sus la cainne de la gorge, et ne touchier la gorge mais la remet selonc sa figure naturel;	cut the artery above the adam's apple, but do not touch the throat; simply reset it to its natural position;
et puis l’estrain avenanment, et le laisse aucuns jors, puis le cure d’oignemens desechans tant qu’il soit sanez;	then gently pull on it and leave it for several days, then treat the wound with purifying ointments until it is healed;
et se li plaie a fait empression en l’os, si la quier;	and if the wound has made an impression on the bone, then cut it;
et s’il i a pieces d’os, si les trai fuers toz se tu pues, et ces que tu ne pues avoir, si laisse tant que li plaie porrisse,	and if there are pieces of bone, you should draw them all out if you can, and those that you cannot reach, leave them until the wound can heal.
et soit desevree et aligie li issue;	and the joint should be freed and aligned to allow movement.
et se li plaie est fresche, si poudre sus la poudre que j’ai dit.	and if the wound is fresh, apply the powder I have described.
Et s’il a en la plaie os et il i a fistule, si la cure ensi com j’ai dit en son chapistre.	And if there is bone in the wound and there is a fistula, treat it as I have described in its chapter.
de la plaie de lance ou de coutel	of a wound from a spear or knife
Se c’est cop de lance ou de coutel, et li plaie est parfonde, si regarde se de la plaie saut ventositez cant li malaides alainne: saiches adonques que li plaie est mortelz;	If it is a spear or knife wound and the wound is deep, then examine if the wound is bleeding profusely: know therefore that the wound is lethal;
et s’elle n’est parfonde, et elle est fresche a tout son sanc, si n’i mettre mie a la premiere houre la poudre, ne ne la liier mie por le sanc que ne demorse em parfont,	and it is not deep, and it is fresh with all its blood, then do not put the powder in at first or ligature it for the bleeding will stop on its own,
et reviegne au cuer, et ocie lou malaide;	and heal the patient;
mais i met oignement atractif, et le lie .ij. fois le jor;	but I apply an attractive ointment, and bind it .ii. times a day;
et se tu n’as oignement, si met en la plaie viel coton por succier fuers la moistor,	and if you do not have ointment, then put old cotton in the wound to suck out moisture,
et fai dormir le malaide sus la plaie .iij. jors, ou .iiij., ou plusors;	and let the patient sleep on the wound for 3 or 4, or more days;
si n’i venra mie spasme, ne tremor male de cuer n’es traingnemens d’alainne;	if there is no twitching, nor trembling of the heart, nor shaking chills;
et quant tu vois les bones dispositions, si saiches que li plaie est sauve.	and when you see the bones in good alignment, then you know that the wound is healed.
Cure la donques de tentes et d’autres cures, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Treat it with poultices and other remedies until it is healed;
et s’elle ne puet saner, et oevre, adés saiches que il i a fistule; si la cure si com on doit.	and if it cannot heal, and there is an opening, then you know that there is a fistula; treat it as one should.
Et se li plaie est d’incision d’espee ou de coutel, et elle est simple, ou pis ou au dos, si la cure de ceu qui est devant;	And if the wound is from a sword or knife, and it is simple, or on the front or back, then treat it as one would expect;
s’elle est grans, de cousture; et s’elle est petite, de poudre, et s’elle est empressee en l’os, et en a copeit pieces, si quier la plaie, et les trai fuers s’il sont desevrez;	if it is large, with stitches; and if it is small, with powder, and if it is pressed into the bone, and has broken off pieces, then probe the wound, and pull out the foreign objects if they are dislodged.
et s’il ne sont desevrez, si laisse porrir la plaie, si aligera li estractions;	and if they are not dislodged, let the wound fester, so as to ease the extraction.
et des autres plaies as autres membres est li jugemens si com nos avons dit.	and for other wounds in other limbs, the judgment is as we have said.
dou derrompement dou ventre	from rupturing of the belly
Li derompemens dou ventre est grans et moiens et petis;	There are great, medium, and small ruptures of the belly;
de la grant plaie saut aucune fois li intestine, ou li ners des intestines, par coi li intromission d’aus;	from a great wound sometimes the intestines, or the nerves of the intestines, by which the entrance of air;
et li costure est plus malaisie, et aucune fois vaut pis li petite plaie que li grans,	and the sewing is more difficult, and sometimes the smaller wound is worse than the larger,
por ceu c’on remet plus a poinnes les intestines en, s’on ne les i remet de chaut en chaut;	because one puts the intestines in more frequently when they are cold, if one does not warm them gradually;
por ce que li intestine enflent tantost qu’il sentent le froit, si rentrent plus a poinnes,	for the intestines swell as soon as they feel the cold, they contract more with pain,
et por ceu vaut mues li moieinne plaie, por ceu c’on ramoine mues l’intestine a son leu que as autres .ij.	and therefore it is necessary to massage the soft abdomen, so that the intestines return to their place and not to the others.
Et saiches que li routure dou ventre est selonc .iiij. manieres:	And know that the rupture of the belly occurs in four ways:
les .ij. costures communes avienent en la costure dou ventre,	The two common sutures occur in the suture of the abdomen,
et li costure des autres plaies dou cors et .ij. autres costures propres sont communes as autres plaies;	and the stitching of other wounds on the body, and two other proper stitches are common to other wounds;
et toutevoie elles sont plus propres avec la costure dou ventre, et je dirai une chescune et declairerai.	nevertheless they are more appropriate with the stitch of the belly, and I will say each one and declare.
Je di que quant li plaie est petite, et aucune chose de l’intestine ist fuer,	I say that when the wound is small, and something of the intestine has come out,
et griés chose est dou remettre, ceu est par l’une des .ij. manieres:	and it is easy to fix, either by one of two methods:Quant li plaie est grande et que les intestins sont hors, ou qu’il se puet de leu remere, si doit on adonques faire costure en la plus fine peile qui soit dou corps,
ou por la petitece de la plaie, si com nos avons dit,	or for the smallness of the wound, as we have said,
ou por ce que li intestine est enflez por le froit.	or because the intestines are swollen due to cold.
Et quant il est frois, eschaufez lou en teil maniere:	And when it is cold, warm it in such a way:
moillie une esponge ou .i. mol drapeil en aigue tede soulement,	moisten a sponge or soft cloth with tepid water only,
ou tu cuis en aigue squinant et cipre et spique,	where you cook in squint water and cypress and spike,
et arose l’intestine tant que li enfleure soit ostee;	and boil the intestines until they are swollen;
et aucune fois fait ce vins restraingnans, et est muedre que awe soule por desenfler.	and sometimes makes this restraining wine, and is mud that soothes to reduce swelling.
Et quant tu vois l’enfleure departir, si amoiste l’intestine d’aigue ou altee et malves soient cuites,	And when you see the swelling departing, then boil the intestines in water or alt, and let them be cooked
car par ceu est aligie li entree a poc de chose;	for this constricts the entrance to a small degree;
et s’il n’i puet entrer, si fent un poc la plaie a l’estrument de coi on cope les emorroydes;	and if it cannot enter, they make a small wound with the instrument used for cutting hemorrhoids;
et li premiere cure est muedre que li taille,	and the first treatment is more painful than the incision,
que nus n’i doit taillier sens grant necessiteit n’i ait;	which one should not cut without great necessity;
et c’est li estrumens por le fendre:	and this is the instrument for splitting it open:
si trenche dedens en la corbeure et defuer non, et vez ci la forme:	if you cut inside the curve and out again, and look at the shape here:
Et quant li plaie est enlargie, et li intestine saut fuer,	And when the wound is enlarged, and the intestines jump out,
si le remet arer selonc la forme naturel en son leu propre,	if it is reset according to its natural shape in its proper place,
se tu en as pooir, car ce vaut mues.	if you have the power, because this is necessary.
Quant li plaie est large, et elle est en la partie desoz lou ventre,	When the wound is large and it is in the lower part of the abdomen,
si covient que tu faices gesir lou malaide sus son dos,	you should make the patient lie on his back,
et met ses jambes plus haut que son chief;	and put his legs above his head;
et s’elle est en la partie desoz le ventre,	and if it is in the lower part of the belly,
si met le chief et le pis plus haut que les parties desoz,	place the head and the foot higher than the parts below,
et ausi se li routure dou ventre est en l’une des .ij. parties	and also if the rupture in the belly is in one of the two parts,
si met t’entente en ceu que li partie navree soit plus haute que li autre;	place it so that the ruptured part is higher than the other;
et ensi covient amenistrer ceu que je dis en plaies grans et moienes.	and thus one must treat those things which I say about large and small wounds.
Es plaies petites met ceu que t’est apparilliet,	For small wounds, put on what you have prepared,
puis aies entre tes mains .i. ministre pitous ki teigne toute la routure a sa main,	then have at hand a minister who holds the wound open with one hand,
et assemble les levres;	and gathers the lips;
et c’est la maniere commune de costures,	and this is the common way of sewing.
et est que tu preignes une aguille ou plusors, selonc la quantiteit de la largesce de la plaie,	take a needle or several, depending on the width of the wound,
puis laisse des le chief de la plaie .i. doi d’espaice, et i fiche une aguille ou il ait .i. boin fil fort;	then leave about an inch of space from the edge of the wound, and thread a needle with a strong thread;
et perce les .ij. chiés dou cuir avec les .ij. chiés dou siphac,	and pierce the two sides of the skin with the two sides of the wound,
qui est desoz le cuir dedens, tant que tu la faices percier de celle partie,	which is under the skin inside, until you cause it to pierce from that part,
et assemble les .ij. chief dou siphac les .iiij. ensamble;	and join the two heads of the needle, then the four together;
puis l’estrain d’un fil double entor l’aguille de .ij. pars,	then draw it through with a double thread around the needle in two parts,
puis assemble les .ij. chiés de la plaie avenanment,	then join the two heads of the wound smoothly,
et puis laisse .i. doi d’espaice, et i fiche une autre aguille;	and then leave .I. space, and stick another needle;
puis la lie dou fil si com tu as fait la premiere aguille,	then tie the thread as you did with the first needle,
et ne cesser de ceu faire selonc ceu que tu as mestier des aguilles,	and do not stop doing this according to what you need of needles,
tant que toute li plaie soit restrainte;	until all the wound is restrained;The following text is a medieval medical treatise written in Old French, around the 12th-13th centuries.
et soient les aguilles moienes, entre subtilz et grosses,	and let the needles be medium, between fine and thick,
car les aguilles subtilz copent toute la char, et les trop grosses si ne pueent mie bien entrer:	for the fine needles pierce through all the flesh, but the very thick ones cannot enter well.
por ceu covient qu’elles soient moienes;	for this reason they should be medium-sized.
et ne covient mie bouter les aguilles trop au defuer de la char et dou cuir,	and one must not push the needles too deep into the flesh and through the skin,
k’elles ne copent et oevrent la plaie devant la soudure;	so they do not cut and open the wound before the scabs form;
et puis cope les chiés des aguilles, qu’elles ne blecent lou malaide au dormir,	and then cuts the heads of the needles so that they do not prick the patient while sleeping,
et i met tentes ou drapelz au chiés des aguilles por mues tenir,	and puts tents or bandages on the heads of the needles to hold them in place,
et les laisse tant que li plaie soit soudee;	and leaves them until the wound is healed;
et ceste maniere de costure as aguilles est plus covenauble en petites plaies,	and this method of stitching with needles is more suitable for small wounds,
car il i soffist une aguille ou .ij.	because you only need one or two needles.
Li seconde costure si est commune,	The second stitch is common,
et est que tu assemble les .ij. chiés dou cuir et les .ij. chiés dou syfac ensamble a une aguille ou il ait .i. fort fil moien;	and it is to join the two edges of the skin and the two edges of the wound with one needle and a strong thread;
et quant tu avras perciez ces chiez toz .iiij. ensamble,	and when you have cut all four of these nerves together,
si ramoinne l’aguille a la partie ou tu as encomenciet, en la maniere c’on cout les dras;	then remove the needle from the part where you began, in the manner that one sews clothes;
et met d’espaice entre chescune costure la grossece d’un menor doi;	and place a distance between each stitch equal to the thickness of a thumb nail;
ceste costure sevent li home,	this stitch is for men,
et je cousi une plaie c’uns hons avoit ou ventre,	and I sewed up a wound that a man had on his belly,
qui estoit navrez d’un coutel,	which he had received from a knife,
et estoit li plaie plus d’une palme de grant,	and the wound was more than a palm in length,
et issoit des intestines bien .ij. palmes de grant,	and the intestines protruded more than .ij. palms in length,
et estoit li plaie enmi le ventre.	and the wound was in his belly.
Je li ramenai l’intestine puis k’il ot esteit .xxiiij. houres fuer,	I returned his intestines to him then after he had been without them for 24 hours
et fut li plaie soudee jusc’a .xv. jors, et le curai, et fut sanez.	and the wound was sewn up until the 15th day, and I healed it, and he recovered.
Et li mire l’avoient jugiet qu’il morroit, et ce fut miracle;	And they had judged that he would die, and this was a miracle;
et ne le curai mie d’oignement, car je estoie en .i. leu ou on n’en trovoit point, ne nule medicines;	and I didn't treat it with ointments because I was in a place where there were no such things as ointments or medicine to be found;
et metoie sens plus sus la plaie coton viel .ij. fois le jor, et le lavoie d’aigue de miel tant qu’il fut sanez.	and I placed clean cotton on the wound twice a day and washed it with honey water until it healed.
Or vos dirai les .ij. propres manieres de cousture:	Now I will tell you about two proper methods of suturing:
pren l’aguille, et la boute des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens;	take the needle and pierce it through from the outside just up to the inside;
quant elle a perciet le keur de droit en droit, si lai le chief dou siphac ou cousteit ou tu as bouteit l’aguille,	when it has pierced the heart directly, then take out the needle and put in the tube where you have inserted the needle.
et la fai percier d’autre part des la partie dedens jusc’a celi defuer;	then pierce it from another angle to the other side of the body, until it reaches the outside.
et li entendemens de ceste costure si est que tu cous ausi com li peletier font les pelz,	and the technique for this stitching is that you sew as a tailor sews clothes,
et que tu laisses une fois le syfac d’une part, et le reprent d’autre, tant que li costure soit toute acomplie.	and leave the syringe on one side, and pull it from the other, until the stitching is complete.
Li seconde maniere de costure, que Galiens dist proprement,	The second method of stitching, which Galen describes properly,
si est si com aucun font, qui assemblent les .ij. parties ensamble naturelment,	if it is like when two pieces are joined together naturally,
et apploient l’un des chief dou syfac a l’autre chief, en teil maniere:	and the end of one piece to the other end, in such a way that:
fiche une aguille ou chief dou mirach prochiene, et fai percier celui leu soulement,	they pierce through the nearest part of the skin with a needle, and only pierce through that layer,
et laisse les .ij. chiés dou syfac;	and leave the two heads of the sinus;
puis torne l’aguille, et la fai percier des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens,	then turn the needle and pierce it from the outside inwards to the inside,
as .ij. chiés dou syfac;	as the two heads of the sinus;
puis fai percier l’un et l’autre des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens, en .ij. autres chiés dou mirach que sont on l’autre costeit;	then pierce one and then the other from the outside inwards to the inside, in two other heads of the sinus that are on the other side;
et c’est li muedre maniere de costure et li plus commune.	and this is the mother of stitches and the most common.
Galiens si dist ceste parolle, et aucun le tesmoignent,	Galen says these words, and some testify to it,
c’on doit coudre le ventre a .ij. aguilles, ou il ait fil en chescune;	one must sew the belly with .2 needles, having thread in each;
et doit on bouter l’une aguille d’une part, et l’autre d’autre, en la maniere de ces qui cousent corroies;	and one needle from one side and the other from the other, in the manner of those who sew腐;
et saiches que quant li routure est enmi lou ventre,	and you know that when a hernia is in the abdomen,
si est li cousture plus griez que des autres leus dou ventre.	the incision should be made larger than other places in the abdomen.
Li jugemens de la plaie si est telz com li jugemens des autres plaies:	The judgment of the wound is the same as the judgment of other wounds:
et est que quant tu trueves la plaie fresche a tout son sanc, ainsois que li ars l’ait muee,	and it is that when you find the fresh wound with all its blood, as long as the flesh has not moved,
si remet arer l’intestine, et lou cout; puis met sus la poudre enjanrant char,	if one replaces the intestines and sutures them; then place the charred powder on top,
et se li ars l’ait muee, si met sus aucun oignement que soit present, tant que li plaie bowe;	and if it burns, then put any ointment that is available on the wound until it heals;
et chicent li fil, et soient soudez li sifac, et li mirach;	and tie the thread, and sew the intestines, and the membrane;
puis cure la plaie si com les autres, tant qu’il soit sanez;	then treat the wound as with the others until it is healed;The following text is a medieval medical treatise written in Old French, around the 12th-13th centuries.
et se tu n’as medicines, si met sus, tantost qu’ele comance a giter bowe, coton viel,	and if you have no medicine, place old cotton
et le remue .ij. fois le jor tant k’il soit sanez.	and move it twice a day until it is healed.
Car tu n’as mestier d’autre medicine en plusors dispositions cant les plaies sont simples;	For in various wounds, you don't need any other medicine;
et se tu doutes que li plaie ne faice communiteit as membres principelz,	and if you doubt that the wound causes corruption in the principal members,

Li intestine qui est apelez «jeun» ne puet saner quant il est navrez,	The intestine which is called "young" cannot heal when it is raw,
et c’est por la planteit des voinnes que i sont, et por la subtiliteit de tout le cors, et l’aprochement de sa nature des ners.	and it's because of the thinness of the veins that they are, and because of the subtlety of the whole body, and its proximity to the nerves.

de la routure dou boueil	of the rot of boiling water
Quant li intestine est rons, et li plaie est petite,	When the intestines are torn, and the wound is small,
si la puet on restorer en aucuns homes,	one can restore it in some ways,
por ceu que je vis que uns hons fut navrez ou ventre d’une lance;	because I saw a man who was pierced in the belly with a lance;he had a wound that was about a span long, and it was very deep. He was dead before he could be healed.
et estoit li plaie au destre de l’estomac,	and the wound was on the right side of the stomach,
et fut envillie et devint fistule, et en issoit li egestion et li ventositez;	and it became a fistula, and from it came the evacuations and the flatulence;
je i mis cure selonc ceu que je poi, et ne cessai de subtilier tant qu’il fut sanez, et li leus soudez.	I treated it with salt according to what I could, and I did not cease to cauterize until it was healed and the wounds closed.
Et quant je le vis souder, je doutai que li malaides n’eust mal en son ventre;	And when I saw it healing, I feared that the patient had discomfort in his abdomen;The following text is a medieval medical treatise written in Old French, around the 12th-13th centuries.
et il n’i ot point de mal, mais demora en millors dispositions, et menjans et bevans;	and there was no harm done, but he remained in better condition, eating and drinking;
et dirent aucun experimentors que quant il a petite plaie en l’intestine, qu’il doit estre liiez en teil maniere:	and some expérimentors say that when there is a small wound in the intestines, it must be bound in such a way:

Cil chief si s’aerdent en l’intestine, et ne vient nulle nuisance au malaide,	If they get stuck in the intestines and do not harm the patient,
et se puet on liier l’intestine d’un fil subtil qui est copez de l’intestine d’une beste,	and one can tie the intestine with a thin thread that is cut from the intestine of an animal,

de fistule ou qu’ele soit	of a fistula, wherever it may be
Saiches que toute plaie ou aposteme, quant il enveillist, si est apelee universement «fistule»,	You should know that any wound or abscess, when it breaks open, is universally called a "fistula",
et meismement quant elle est chevee et rent bowe.	and especially when it is deep and narrow.
Et fistule est selonc la verteit nodation fautree dure et blainche, ou on ne sent dolor,	A fistula is a hard, white, knotted swelling without pain,
et est ausi chevee com li penne d’un oiseil;	it has a head like the beak of a bird;
et aucune fois en saut clere bowe, et autre fois espesse;	sometimes it is thin and clear, sometimes thick;
aucune fois poc, et autre fois assez;	sometimes little, sometimes enough;
et je en ai jai parleit en la division des plaies, que toute plaie que n’est sanee, et il n’i a char,	and I have spoken of this in the division of wounds, that any wound that is not healed and there is no scar,
ce n’est fuers que par une des .viiij. causes:	it is caused by none of the .viiij. causes:
c’est a savoir, par la petitece dou sanc ou cors;	that is to say, by the little-ness of blood or body;
ou por sa malice;	or because of its wickedness;
ou por ceu qu’il i a char dure dedens, et sus les levres, que n’i laisse naistre char;	or because there is hard flesh within it and on the lips that does not let flesh grow;
ou il i a trop de bowe;	or where there is too much bowing;
ou li leus est porris, et li matiere est de male qualiteit;	or the bones are porous and the material of poor quality;
ou li medicine n’est mie bone en la cure;	or the medicine is not good for the treatment;
ou por ceu que li corruption est maniere de pestilence;	or because the infection is a form of pestilence;
ou por la proprieteit en la region est tardive li digestion, et tarde li santeit, et enflee par nature;	or because of the nature of the region is late digestion, and slow health, and swollen by nature;
ou il i a voinnes ou os:	or there are veins or bones:
et j’ai ja mostreit toutes ces causes, et les signes, et les cures de medicines en la division.	and I have already shown all these causes, and the signs, and the remedies of medicine in the division.
Or covient que je te faice a savoir la cure de fistule qui est faite par oevre de mains.	Now I should let you know about the treatment of fistula which is done by handiwork.
Saiches que fistule avient en tous membres dou cors;	Know that fistulas occur in all parts of the body;
car il i a fistules que vienent as grans voines, et as arteres, et as ners,	for there are fistulas that come from large veins, and from arteries, and from nerves,
ou au syfac, ou a l’intestine, ou a la vessie, ou a aucunes des costes,	or in the sinus, or in the intestines, or in the bladder, or in some of the ribs,
ou a l’espinee dou dos, ou a aucune jointe des mains ou des piez;	or in the spine of the back, or in any joint of the hands or feet;The following text is a medieval medical treatise written in Old French, around the 12th-13th centuries.
et si a teil que vient a la proprieteit dou membre principeil, et as semblans leus.	and if it affects the principal organ, and similar places.
Et toutes les fistules que sont de ceste maniere sont de grief sanation, et n’i a fors que labour, et ignorance;	And all fistulas that are in this way are grievous to heal, and there is nothing but labor and ignorance;
et se il i a aucune fistule que ne veigne mie jusc’a leu que j’ai dit, et tu as fiance de la cure,	and if there is any fistula that does not come to the place I have described, and you are confident in its treatment,
et tu la vues conoistre, si pren une tente d’arain ou de fer, se li fistule est droite, si la quier;	and you see it, take an iron or bronze tent, if the fistula is straight, so take it;
et se li fistule est torte, si la cerche d’une subtil tente de plonc,	and if the fistula is crooked, then search for a subtle thread of pus
car li plons se ploie mues entor la tortuositeit;	because the pus bends around the crookedness;
et se li fistule a mains pertus et tu ne la pues mie bien cerchier par tentes,	and if the fistula has many openings and you cannot well search it with threads,
si la clisterize par l’un des pertus,	if you cleanse it through one of the openings,
car la moistors si cort d’un pertus a autre, et la mundifie;	for moisture cuts from one pore to another, and cleanses.
